I hear a voice, Illmuire? "[i]Don't you recognize yourself?[/i]" she asks.

Her name is ... Nero?

[i]You too?[/i]

(The hero is overwhelmed. We take him now, we'll have him now... Oh 'my' what a special gift. We have plans.)

(He would live many lives. As a Vixen he had a cult, as a farmer he became a vixen's pet, as a War Chief he became... terrible, wonderful. He returned to this time, this place, devouring Dread. [i]Many times[/i]. And... through this multitude of experience, fornicating, he becomes more.)

It's not over -> Next chapter "Recreation"
